```json
    {"step": "Shift the y-coordinates down by the calculated value", "condition": "if the color is the one that gets shifted and the new y-coordinate is less than the original y-coordinate"},
    {"step": "Leave the object unchanged", "condition": "if the color is the one that doesn't get shifted"}
  ]
}
```
Note: In the `transformation_steps`, the condition mentioned in step 2 is dependent on the specific example and the overall pattern, so it needs to be adjusted accordingly. Also, step 3 has multiple conditions combined using `and`.#############################

   * Shift the y-coordinates down by the calculated value if the new y-coordinate is less than the original y-coordinate.
3. Leave objects with color 1 unchanged.
